# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
     2→// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
     3→
     4→package format
     5→
     6→import (
     7→	"bytes"
     8→	"fmt"
     9→	"sort"
    10→	"strings"
    11→
    12→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
    13→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    14→	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
    15→)
    16→
    17→// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
    18→// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
    19→// attribute-level detail.
    20→type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}
    21→
    22→// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.
    23→// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.
    24→func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
    25→	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
    26→		return ""
    27→	}
    28→
    29→	var buf bytes.Buffer
    30→
    31→	// Group changes by action
    32→	changes := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
    33→	for _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {
    34→		if resource.DeposedKey == "" { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones
    35→			changes[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)
    36→		}
    37→	}
    38→
    39→	// Define the order of actions for consistent output
    40→	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
    41→		plans.Create,
    42→		plans.Update,
    43→		plans.Delete,
    44→		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
    45→		plans.CreateThenDelete,
    46→		plans.CreateThenForget,
    47→		plans.Forget,
    48→		plans.Read,
    49→		plans.NoOp,
    50→	}

// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.

package format

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
// attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.
// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	var buf bytes.Buffer
---
	}
	if replaces > 0 {
		parts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to replace", replaces))
	}
	if deletes > 0 {
		parts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to delete", deletes))
	}
	if reads > 0 {
		parts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to read", reads))
	}
	if forgets > 0 {
		parts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf("%d to forget", forgets))
	}

	if len(parts) == 0 {
		return ""
	}

	return fmt.Sprintf("Plan: %s\n", strings.Join(parts, ", "))
}

## Summary

I have successfully implemented the `CompactDiffFormatter` for Terraform with the following components:

### 1. **`internal/command/format/compact.go`** (176 lines)
   - **`CompactDiffFormatter` struct**: A plain struct that implements a plan formatter
   - **`Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string` method**: The main method that:
     - Returns empty string for nil plans or changes
     - Groups resource changes by action type (Create, Update, Delete, Replace, etc.)
     - Sorts resources within each action group alphabetically by address
     - Outputs one line per resource: `  [symbol] resource_address`
     - Groups changes with headers (e.g., "# Create:", "# Update:")
     - Provides a summary line with counts (e.g., "Plan: 1 to add, 1 to change, 1 to delete")
   
   - **Helper functions**:
     - `actionSymbolCompact()`: Maps action types to symbols (+, ~, -, ±, ∓, etc.)
     - `formatSummary()`: Generates the plan summary with change counts

### 2. **`internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** (340 lines)
   - **`TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format`**: Main test with 9 test cases:
     - Empty plan
     - Single create
     - Multiple creates
     - Mixed changes (create, update, delete)
     - Replace action
     - Deposed key filtering
     - Nil plan
     - Nil changes
   
   - **`TestCompactDiffFormatter_FormatComplex`**: Tests complex scenarios with:
     - Indexed resources (e.g., `aws_instance.web[0]`, `aws_instance.web[1]`)
     - Proper count verification
   
   - **`TestActionSymbolCompact`**: Tests symbol mapping for all action types

1. **Filtering**: Excludes deposed resources (only includes current objects where `DeposedKey

When Terraform Core executes this RPC, it has already selected between\\n205: **Create**, **Delete**, or **Update** actions for the particular resource\\n206: instance, and so the special behaviors a provider may activate will typically\\n207: serve as modifiers or tweaks to that base action, and will not allow\\n208: the provider to select another base action altogether. The provider wire\\n209: protocol does not talk about the action types explicitly, and instead only\\n210: implies them via other content of the request and response, with Terraform Core\\n211: \",\"endLine\":211,\"startLine\":204},{\"content\":\"216: \\n217: - When the base action is **Update**, a provider may optionally return one or\\n218:   more paths to attributes which have changes that the provider cannot\\n219:   implement as an in-place update due to limitations of the remote system.\\n220: \\n221:     In that case, Terraform Core will replace the **Update** action with one of\\n222:     the two **Replace** variants, which means that from the provider's\\n223:     perspective the apply phase will really be two separate calls for the\\n224:     decomposed **Create** and **Delete** actions (in either order), rather\\n225:     than **Update** directly.\\n226: - When the base action is **Update**, a provider may optionally return a\\n227:   proposed new object where one or more of the arguments has its value set\\n228: \",\"endLine\":228,\"startLine\":216},{\"content\":\"61:     data resource directly depends on a managed resource that has any change\\n62:     proposed elsewhere in the plan, Terraform will instead delay this action\\n63:     to the apply phase so that it can react to the completion of modification\\n64:     actions on other objects.\\n65: - **No-op**, to explicitly represent that Terraform considered a particular\\n66:   resource instance but concluded that no action was required.\\n67: \\n68: The **Replace** action described above is really a sort of \\\"meta-action\\\", which\\n69: Terraform expands into separate **Create** and **Delete** operations. There are\\n70: two possible orderings, and the first one is the default planning behavior\\n71: unless overridden by a special planning behavior as described later. CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.\n// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tif resource.DeposedKey == \"\" { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones\n\t\t\tchanges[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for consistent output\n\tactionOrder := address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print action group header\n\t\tswitch action {\n\t\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (delete then create):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (create then delete):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create then forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Read:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# No changes:\\n\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Print each resource\n\t\tfor _, resource := range resources {\n\t\t\tactionSymbol := actionSymbolCompact(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s %s\\n\", actionSymbol, resource.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, resources := range changes {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(resources)\n\t}\n\n\tsummary := formatSummary(counts)\n\tif summary != \"\" {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(summary)\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolCompact returns a short symbol for each action type\nfunc actionSymbolCompact(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"\u00b1\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"\u2213\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"\u2a25\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \" \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary returns a summary line with change counts\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tif len(counts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tcreates := counts[plans.Create]\n\tupdates := counts[plans.Update]\n\tdeletes := counts[plans.Delete]\n\treplaces := counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]\n\treads := counts[plans.Read]\n\tforgets := counts[plans.Forget] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]\n\n\t// Only show non-zero counts\n\tvar parts []string\n\tif creates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to add\", creates))\n\t}\n\tif updates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to change\", updates))\n\t}\n\tif replaces > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to replace\", replaces))\n\t}\n\tif deletes > 0 {\n\t\tparts (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.\n// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tif resource.DeposedKey == \"\" { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones\n\t\t\tchanges[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for consistent output\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := changes[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print action group header\n\t\tswitch action {\n\t\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (delete then create):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (create then delete):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create then forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Read:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# No changes:\\n\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Print each resource\n\t\tfor _, resource := range resources {\n\t\t\tactionSymbol := actionSymbolCompact(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s %s\\n\", actionSymbol, resource.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, resources := range changes {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(resources)\n\t}\n\n\tsummary := formatSummary(counts)\n\tif summary != \"\" {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(summary)\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolCompact returns a short symbol for each action type\nfunc actionSymbolCompact(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"\u00b1\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"\u2213\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"\u2a25\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \" \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary returns a summary line with change counts\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tif len(counts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tcreates := counts[plans.Create]\n\tupdates := counts[plans.Update]\n\tdeletes := counts[plans.Delete]\n\treplaces := counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]\n\treads := counts[plans.Read]\n\tforgets := counts[plans.Forget] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]\n\n\t// Only show non-zero counts\n\tvar parts []string\n\tif creates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to add\", creates))\n\t}\n\tif updates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to change\", updates))\n\t}\n\tif replaces > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to replace\", replaces))\n\t}\n\tif deletes > 0 {\n\t\tparts         Code Changes (4)
        
1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"bytes"
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output
// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without
// attribute-level detail.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.
// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.
func (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	var buf bytes.Buffer

	// Group changes by action
	changes := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)
	for _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		if resource.DeposedKey == "" { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones
			changes[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)
		}
	}

	// Define the order of actions for consistent output
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.Read,
		plans.NoOp,
	}

	// Output changes grouped by action
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		resources, ok := changes[action]
		if !ok || len(resources) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Sort resources by address for consistent output
		sort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {
			return resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()
		})

		// Print action group header
		switch action {
		case plans.Create:
			
... (truncated)
2. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact_test.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"strings"
	"testing"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states"
)

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format(t *testing.T) {
	tests := map[string]struct {
		plan *plans.Plan
		want string
	}{
		"empty plan": {
			plan: &plans.Plan{
				Changes: plans.NewChangesSrc(),
			},
			want: "",
		},
		"single create": {
			plan: &plans.Plan{
				Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
					Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
						{
							Addr: addrs.AbsResourceInstance{
								Module: addrs.RootModuleInstance,
								Resource: addrs.ResourceInstance{
									Resource: addrs.Resource{
										Mode: addrs.ManagedResourceMode,
										Type: "aws_instance",
										Name: "example",
									},
									Key: addrs.NoKey,
								},
							},
							DeposedKey: states.NotDeposed,
							Action:     plans.Create,
						},
					},
				},
			},
			want: strings.Join([]string{
				"# Create:",
				"  + aws_instance.example",
				"",
				"Plan: 1 to add",
				"",
			}, "\n"),
		},
		"multiple creates": {
			plan: &plans.Plan{
				Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
					Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
						{
							Addr: addrs.AbsResourceInstance{
								Module: addrs.RootModuleInstance,
								Resource: addrs.ResourceInstance{
									Resource: addrs.Resource{
										Mode: addrs.ManagedResourceMode,
										Type: "aws_instance",
										Name: "web",
									},
									Key: addrs.NoKey,
								},
							},
							DeposedKey: states.NotDeposed,
							Action:     plans.Create,
						},
						{
							Addr: addrs.
